</a> </div> </div> </div> </div> </div> </div> <span class="author-timestamp" content="2019-08-29T01:48-500" itemprop="datePublished">August 29</span> </div> <p data-elm-loc="0">The next Democratic debate will treat viewers to a spectacle unseen this cycle — all of the qualifying candidates debating on the same stage, on the same night.</p> <p data-elm-loc="1">The debate, set for Thursday, Sept. 12, would continue the next night <a href="https://abcnews.go.com/Politics/abc-news-announces-details-democratic-primary-debate/story?id=65077321" target="_blank">only if more than 10 candidates qualify</a>. Exactly 10 candidates made the cut.</p> <p data-elm-loc="2">To qualify, candidates had to register at least 2 percent in four of the 21 qualifying polls and earn donations from at least 130,000 individuals by Wednesday, Aug. 28.</p> <div class="inline-content inline-html" data-elm-loc="3"> <style media="screen,print" defer="">(function(containerId,opts){if(!("querySelector"in document))return;var container=document.getElementById(containerId);var nameSpace=opts.namespace||"";var onResize=throttle(update,200);var waiting=!!window.IntersectionObserver;var observer;update();document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded",update);window.addEventListener("resize",onResize);if(opts.setup)opts.setup(container).on("cleanup",cleanup);function cleanup(){document.removeEventListener("DOMContentLoaded",update);window.removeEventListener("resize",
onResize);if(observer)observer.disconnect()}function update(){var artboards=selectChildren("."+nameSpace+"artboard[data-min-width]",container),width=Math.round(container.getBoundingClientRect().width);artboards.forEach(function(el){var minwidth=el.getAttribute("data-min-width"),maxwidth=el.getAttribute("data-max-width");if(+minwidth<=width&&(+maxwidth>=width||maxwidth===null)){if(!waiting)selectChildren("."+nameSpace+"aiImg",el).forEach(updateImgSrc);el.style.display="block"}else el.style.display=
"none"});if(waiting&&!observer)if(elementInView(container)){waiting=false;update()}else{observer=new IntersectionObserver(onIntersectionChange,{});observer.observe(container)}}function elementInView(el){var bounds=el.getBoundingClientRect();return bounds.top<window.innerHeight&&bounds.bottom>0}function updateImgSrc(img){var src=img.getAttribute("data-src");if(src&&img.getAttribute("src")!=src)img.setAttribute("src",src)}function onIntersectionChange(entries){if(entries.length&&entries[0].isIntersecting){waiting=

setup:window.setupInteractive||window.getComponent});</script> </div> <p data-elm-loc="4">The more stringent rules that the Democratic National Committee <a href="https://democrats.org/news/third-debate/" target="_blank">laid out for the third debate</a> were an attempt to narrow the historically large field. Five candidates dropped out of the race in July and August: Rep. Eric Swalwell (D-Calif.), former Colorado governor John Hickenlooper, Washington Gov. Jay Inslee, Rep. Seth Moulton (D-Mass.) and Sen. Kirsten Gillibrand (D-N.Y.). But 20 remain in the race.</p> <p data-elm-loc="5">Candidates on the bubble have missed their chance this round.
